Puede cargar y abrir dibujos DWG 2D directamente desde la unidad de disco duro, el correo electrónico o un dispositivo de almacenamiento externo y ver todos los aspectos del archivo DWG, como las referencias externas, las capas y los calcos subyacentes de imagen. Actualice a la versión Premium de la aplicación para dispositivos móviles de AutoCAD a fin de activar las herramientas de edición y dibujo. Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it.
